区卫标准化接口文档

（药品、物资、耗材）

V1.0

2023年09月

版本信息：

| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |

**通用说明：**

1. 本章各业务接口说明中的请求参数和返回参数只包含对应服务参数中具体业务参数段的部分。

# 药品进销存数据接口详情示例

## A4001商品盘存上传

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **A4001** | | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **A4001商品盘存上传（V1.0）** | | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/drug/GetInventoryInfo** | | | | | |
| **功能简述** | **根据开始、结束时间及机构查询所有药品盘点数据信息** | | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | | |
| 1. 查询药品盘点信息。 2. 适用于三方系统进行新增盘点数据 | | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "org\_id": "",  "start\_time": "",  "end\_time": ""  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| start\_time |  | string | **√** | |  | 开始时间 |
| end\_time |  | string | **√** | |  | 结束时间 |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "code": "200",  "msg": "查询商品盘存上传信息成功！",  "data": [  {  "prod\_stoin\_id": "5013090517888055513",  "prod\_type": 1,  "med\_list\_codg": "280103",  "fixmedins\_hilist\_id": "zlsoft",  "fixmedins\_hilist\_name": "中联区卫",  "rx\_flag": "",  "invdate": "2023-08-21 11:28:11",  "ord\_no": "2308000002",  "inv\_cnt": 1,  "pric": 19,  "spler\_code": null,  "spler\_name": null,  "manu\_lotnum": "",  "batch\_number": "0",  "fixmedins\_bchno": "0(307-2308000002)",  "manu\_date": null,  "expy\_end": null,  "storageroomname": "测试药房",  "stockstatus": 1,  "memo": ""  }  ]  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **数组** | **说明** | | |
| code |  | int |  | 返回结果: 200-成功; 500-失败 | | |
| msg |  | string |  | 返回信息 | | |
| data |  |  |  | 执行结果: 返回查询的盘点信息数据 | | |
| prod\_stoin\_id | data | string |  | 商品入库记录主键, 院内惟一 | | |
| prod\_type | data | int |  | 商品类型1、药品2、耗材、3、器械 | | |
| med\_list\_codg | data | string |  | 医疗目录编码 | | |
| fixmedins\_hilist\_id | data | string |  | 定点医药机构目录编号 | | |
| fixmedins\_hilist\_name | data | string |  | 定点医药机构目录名称 | | |
| rx\_flag | data | string |  | 处方药标志 | | |
| invdate | data | string |  | 盘存日期 | | |
| ord\_no | data | string |  | 订单号,如在省公共资源交易中心采购-订单号，否则不用 | | |
| inv\_cnt | data | number |  | 库存数量,按最小计价包装单位统计 | | |
| pric | data | number |  | 单价 | | |
| spler\_code | data | string |  | 供应商编码,指配送企业编码 | | |
| spler\_name | data | string |  | 供应商名称,指配送企业名称 | | |
| manu\_lotnum | data | string |  | 生产批号 | | |
| batch\_number | data | string |  | 批次号,同品、同批用作销售的 | | |
| fixmedins\_bchno | data | string |  | 定点医药机构批次流水号,医药机构自定义批次号 | | |
| manu\_date | data | string |  | 生产日期 | | |
| expy\_end | data | string |  | 有效期止 | | |
| storageroomname | data | string |  | 库房名称 | | |
| stockstatus | data | int |  | 库存状态,库存状态，1 正常、2 缺货、3 停止挂网 | | |
| memo | data | string |  | 备注 | | |

## A4002商品库存变更

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **A4002** | | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **A4002商品库存变更（V1.0）** | | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/drug/GetStockChangeInfo** | | | | | |
| **功能简述** | **根据开始、结束时间及机构查询药品库存变更信息** | | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | | |
| 1、查询药品变更信息。  2、适用于三方系统进行新增药品变更数据 | | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "org\_id": "",  "start\_time": "",  "end\_time": ""  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| start\_time |  | string | **√** | |  | 开始时间 |
| end\_time |  | string | **√** | |  | 结束时间 |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "code": "200",  "msg": "查询商品库存变更信息成功！",  "data": [  {  "med\_list\_codg": "100000100801",  "inv\_chg\_type": "1",  "fixmedins\_hilist\_id": "zlsoft",  "fixmedins\_hilist\_name": "中联区卫",  "fixmedins\_bchno": "20230413170544001(1-2309000001)",  "pric": 11.5,  "cnt": 0,  "rx\_flag": "",  "inv\_chg\_time": "2023-09-01 03:02:04",  "inv\_chg\_opter\_name": "郑静",  "memo": "药品处方新增",  "trdn\_flag": "",  "prod\_stoin\_id": "4862936721226687822",  "inv\_cnt": 999884  }  ]  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **数组** | **说明** | | |
| code |  | int |  | 返回结果: 200-成功; 500-失败 | | |
| msg |  | string |  | 返回信息 | | |
| data |  |  |  | 执行结果: 返回查询的库存变更数据 | | |
| med\_list\_codg | data | string |  | 医疗目录编码 | | |
| inv\_chg\_type | data | string |  | 库存变更类型 | | |
| fixmedins\_hilist\_id | data | string |  | 定点医药机构目录编号 | | |
| fixmedins\_hilist\_name | data | string |  | 定点医药机构目录名称 | | |
| fixmedins\_bchno | data | string |  | 定点医药机构批次流水号 | | |
| pric | data | number |  | 单价 | | |
| cnt | data | number |  | 数量 | | |
| rx\_flag | data | string |  | 处方药标志 | | |
| inv\_chg\_time | data | string |  | 库存变更时间 | | |
| inv\_chg\_opter\_name | data | string |  | 库存变更经办人姓名 | | |
| memo | data | string |  | 备注 | | |
| trdn\_flag | data | string |  | 拆零标志 | | |
| prod\_stoin\_id | data | string |  | 商品入库记录主键,院内唯一；商品入库记录主键,院内唯一 | | |
| inv\_cnt | data | number |  | 变更后库存数量 | | |

## A4003商品采购

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **A4003** | | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **A4003商品采购（V1.0）** | | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/drug/GetInInfo** | | | | | |
| **功能简述** | **根据开始、结束时间及机构查询药品外购入库信息** | | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | | |
| 1、查询外购入库信息。  2、适用于三方系统进行新增外购入库数据 | | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "org\_id": "",  "start\_time": "",  "end\_time": ""  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| start\_time |  | string | **√** | |  | 开始时间 |
| end\_time |  | string | **√** | |  | 结束时间 |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "code": "200",  "msg": "查询商品采购信息成功！",  "data": [  {  "prod\_stoin\_id": "5350082631919029168",  "prod\_type": 1,  "ord\_no": "2308000006",  "med\_list\_codg": "300000140602",  "fixmedins\_hilist\_id": "zlsoft",  "fixmedins\_hilist\_name": "中联区卫",  "dynt\_no": "",  "fixmedins\_bchno": "20230801153005001(301-2308000006)",  "barcode": null,  "purc\_invo\_no\_one": "",  "invoiceseqno\_one": "",  "purc\_invo\_no\_two": "",  "invoiceseqno\_two": "",  "spler\_name": "中联区卫",  "spler\_pmtno": "",  "manu\_lotnum": "002",  "manufacturer": "",  "prodentp\_name": "",  "aprvno": "",  "manu\_date": "2023-07-31 00:00:00",  "expy\_end": "2025-07-31 00:00:00",  "finl\_trns\_pric": 0.6556,  "purc\_retn\_cnt": 40,  "purc\_invo\_codg": "",  "purc\_invo\_no": "",  "rx\_flag": "",  "purc\_retn\_stoin\_time": "2023-08-01 15:30:30",  "inspperson": "管理员",  "inspdate": "2023-08-01 15:30:30",  "spler\_code": "07",  "rxflag": "",  "purc\_retn\_opter\_name": "管理员",  "prod\_geay\_flag": 0,  "memo": ""  }  ]  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **数组** | **说明** | | |
| code |  | int |  | 返回结果: 200-成功; 500-失败 | | |
| msg |  | string |  | 返回信息 | | |
| data |  |  |  | 执行结果: 返回查询的外购入库数据 | | |
| prod\_stoin\_id | data | string |  | 商品入库记录主键, 院内惟一 | | |
| prod\_type | data | string |  | 商品类型 | | |
| ord\_no | data | string |  | 订单号 | | |
| med\_list\_codg | data | string |  | 医疗目录编码 | | |
| fixmedins\_hilist\_id | data | string |  | 定点医药机构目录编号 | | |
| fixmedins\_hilist\_name | data | string |  | 定点医药机构目录名称 | | |
| dynt\_no | data | string |  | 随货单号 | | |
| fixmedins\_bchno | data | string |  | 定点医药机构批次流水号 | | |
| barcode | data | string |  | 商品条码 | | |
| purc\_invo\_no\_one | data | string |  | 一票发票号码 | | |
| invoiceseqno\_one | data | string |  | 一票发票代码 | | |
| purc\_invo\_no\_two | data | string |  | 二票发票号码 | | |
| invoiceseqno\_two | data | string |  | 二票发票代码 | | |
| spler\_name | data | string |  | 供应商名称 | | |
| spler\_pmtno | data | string |  | 供应商许可证号 | | |
| manu\_lotnum | data | string |  | 生产批号 | | |
| manufacturer | data | string |  | 产地 | | |
| prodentp\_name | data | string |  | 生产厂家名称 | | |
| aprvno | data | string |  | 批准文号 | | |
| manu\_date | data | string |  | 生产日期 | | |
| expy\_end | data | string |  | 有效期止 | | |
| finl\_trns\_pric | data | number |  | 最终成交单价 | | |
| purc\_retn\_cnt | data | number |  | 采购/退货数量 | | |
| purc\_invo\_codg | data | string |  | 采购发票编码 | | |
| purc\_invo\_no | data | string |  | 采购发票号 | | |
| rx\_flag | data | string |  | 处方药标志 | | |
| purc\_retn\_stoin\_time | data | string |  | 采购/退货入库时间 | | |
| inspperson | data | string |  | 入库验收员 | | |
| inspdate | data | string |  | 入库验收日期 | | |
| spler\_code | data | string |  | 供应商编码 | | |
| rxflag | data | string |  | 处方药标志 | | |
| purc\_retn\_opter\_name | data | string |  | 采购/退货经办人姓名 | | |
| prod\_geay\_flag | data | string |  | 商品赠送标志 | | |
| memo | data | string |  | 备注 | | |

## A4004商品采购退货

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **A4004** | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **A4004商品采购退货（V1.0）** | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/drug/GetReturnInfo** | | | | |
| **功能简述** | **根据开始、结束时间及机构查询所有药品退库信息** | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | |
| 1、查询药品退库信息。  2、适用于三方系统进行新增退库数据 | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | |
| {  "org\_id": "",  "start\_time": "",  "end\_time": ""  } | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | **数组** | **说明** |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** |  | 机构id |
| start\_time |  | string | **√** |  | 开始时间 |
| end\_time |  | string | **√** |  | 结束时间 |
| **出参示例** | | | | | |
| {  "code": "200",  "msg": "查询商品采购退货信息成功！",  "data": [  {  "med\_list\_codg": "100000100801",  "fixmedins\_hilist\_id": "zlsoft",  "fixmedins\_hilist\_name": "中联区卫",  "fixmedins\_bchno": "0(301-2307000032)",  "spler\_name": "卫材供应商（勿动）",  "spler\_pmtno": "678",  "manu\_lotnum": "20001",  "prodentp\_name": "市制药总厂",  "aprvno": "2001",  "manu\_date": "2023-07-17 00:00:00",  "expy\_end": "2025-04-13 00:00:00",  "finl\_trns\_pric": 11.5,  "purc\_retn\_cnt": -5,  "purc\_invo\_codg": "",  "purc\_invo\_no": null,  "rx\_flag": "",  "purc\_retn\_stoin\_time": "2023-07-17 16:00:35",  "purc\_retn\_opter\_name": "李建中",  "memo": "",  "medins\_prod\_purc\_no": "2307000032",  "prod\_retn\_id": "4743132874745245578",  "prod\_stoin\_id": "4743132874745245578",  "prod\_type": 1,  "ord\_no": "2307000032",  "barcode": null,  "spler\_code": "03",  "manufacturer": "",  "sup\_address": "",  "checkperson": "李建中",  "checkdate": "2023-07-17 16:00:35"  }  ]  } | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **数组** | **说明** | |
| code |  | int |  | 返回结果: 200-成功; 500-失败 | |
| msg |  | string |  | 返回信息 | |
| data |  |  |  | 执行结果: 返回查询的药品退库信息 | |
| med\_list\_codg | data | string |  | 医疗目录编码 | |
| fixmedins\_hilist\_id | data | string |  | 定点医药机构目录编号 | |
| fixmedins\_hilist\_name | data | string |  | 定点医药机构目录名称 | |
| fixmedins\_bchno | data | string |  | 定点医药机构批次流水号 | |
| spler\_name | data | string |  | 供应商名称 | |
| spler\_pmtno | data | string |  | 供应商许可证号 | |
| manu\_lotnum | data | string |  | 生产批号 | |
| prodentp\_name | data | string |  | 生产厂家 | |
| aprvno | data | string |  | 批准文号 | |
| manu\_date | data | string |  | 生产日期 | |
| expy\_end | data | string |  | 有效期止 | |
| finl\_trns\_pric | data | number |  | 最终成交单价 | |
| purc\_retn\_cnt | data | number |  | 采购/退货数量 | |
| purc\_invo\_codg | data | string |  | 采购发票编码 | |
| purc\_invo\_no | data | string |  | 采购发票号 | |
| rx\_flag | data | string |  | 处方药标志 | |
| purc\_retn\_stoin\_time | data | string |  | 采购/退货入库时间 | |
| purc\_retn\_opter\_name | data | string |  | 采购/退货经办人姓名 | |
| memo | data | string |  | 备注 | |
| medins\_prod\_purc\_no | data | string |  | 商品采购流水号 | |
| prod\_retn\_id | data | string |  | 商品退货记录主键, 院内惟一 | |
| prod\_stoin\_id | data | string |  | 商品入库记录主键, 院内惟一 | |
| prod\_type | data | int |  | 商品类型，1、药品2、耗材、3、器械 | |
| ord\_no | data | string |  | 订单号 | |
| barcode | data | string |  | 商品条码 | |
| spler\_code | data | string |  | 供应商编码 | |
| manufacturer | data | string |  | 产地 | |
| sup\_address | data | string |  | 采购退回收货地址 | |
| checkperson | data | string |  | 采购退回出库复核人 | |
| checkdate | data | string |  | 采购退回出库复核日期 | |

## A4005商品销售

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **A4005** | | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **A4005商品销售（V1.0）** | | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/drug/GetSendInfo** | | | | | |
| **功能简述** | **根据开始、结束时间及机构查询所有药品发放信息** | | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | | |
| 1、查询药品发放信息。  2、适用于三方系统进行新增药品发放数据 | | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "org\_id": "",  "start\_time": "",  "end\_time": ""  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| start\_time |  | string | **√** | |  | 开始时间 |
| end\_time |  | string | **√** | |  | 结束时间 |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "code": "200",  "msg": "查询商品销售信息成功！",  "data": [  {  "med\_list\_codg": "0126548",  "fixmedins\_hilist\_id": "zlsoft",  "fixmedins\_hilist\_name": "中联区卫",  "fixmedins\_bchno": "0(310-2301015505)",  "prsc\_dr\_cert\_type": "",  "prsc\_dr\_certno": "",  "prsc\_dr\_name": "管理员",  "phar\_cert\_type": "",  "phar\_certno": "",  "phar\_name": "管理员",  "hi\_feesetl\_type": "",  "setl\_id": "",  "mdtrt\_sn": "2301015505",  "psn\_no": "",  "psn\_cert\_type": "",  "certno": "",  "psn\_name": "长大单",  "manu\_lotnum": "200023",  "manu\_date": "",  "expy\_end": "2022-03-09 00:00:00",  "rx\_flag": "",  "trdn\_flag": 0,  "finl\_trns\_pric": 24,  "rxno": "",  "rx\_circ\_flag": "",  "rtal\_docno": "2301015505",  "stoout\_no": "",  "bchno": "0",  "drug\_trac\_codg": null,  "drug\_prod\_barc": "",  "shelf\_posi": "",  "sel\_retn\_cnt": 9,  "sel\_retn\_time": "2023-01-31 16:03:40",  "sel\_retn\_opter\_name": "管理员",  "memo": "",  "prod\_sal\_id": "5415113437238203522",  "prod\_stoin\_id": "5415113437238203522",  "prod\_type": 1,  "phar\_prac\_cert\_no": null,  "barcode": ""  }  ]  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **数组** | **说明** | | |
| code |  | int |  | 返回结果: 200-成功; 500-失败 | | |
| msg |  | string |  | 返回信息 | | |

## 2.1B3003获取药品信息

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |

## 2.2H1001获取药品库存信息

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **H1001** | | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **H1001获取药品库存信息 （V1.0）** | | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/drug/GetDrugStockInfo** | | | | | |
| **功能简述** | **查询药品库存信息** | | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | | |
| 1、查询药品库存信息。  2、适用于三方系统进行查询药品库存信息 | | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "storehouse\_id":"",  "org\_id":"",  "is\_stock":1,  "drug\_id":"",  "keyword":""  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| storehouse\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 发药库房 |
| is\_stock |  | int | **√** | |  | 是否仅显示有库存数据，1：是，0：否 |
| drug\_id |  | string |  | |  | 药品id，可根据药品id查询 |
| keyword |  | String |  | |  | 关键字，根据药品名称或编码检索药品 |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "code": "200",  "msg": "查询药品信息成功！",  "data": [  {  "id": 800,  "storehouse\_id": "78b7b1988cefddfe",  "drug\_id": "a700898431ce2f1d",  "lot": "20220613191200108",  "lot\_no": "01",  "supplier\_id": null,  "manufacturer": "四川科伦药业股份有限公司",  "sourceland": "",  "approval\_no": "",  "expiry\_date": "2024-06-13 00:00:00",  "occupay\_qty": 0,  "actual\_qty": 153,  "actual\_cost": 682.38,  "actual\_charge": 682.38,  "actual\_spread": 0,  "purchase\_cost": 4.46,  "price": 4.46,  "production\_date": "2022-06-13 00:00:00",  "storehouse": "西药房",  "is\_stop": 0,  "business\_price": null,  "business\_cost\_price": null,  "purchase\_cost\_price": null,  "purchase\_price": null,  "bar\_code": null,  "is\_virtual": 0,  "name": "0.9%氯化钠注射液",  "code": "TP38",  "brand\_name": "",  "strength": "250ml\*2.25g/袋",  "country\_code": "XB05XAL211B002070502180",  "supplier\_name": "中联区卫",  "usable\_qty": 2  }  ]  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **数组** | **说明** | | |
| code |  | int |  | 返回结果: 200-成功; 500-失败 | | |
| msg |  | string |  | 返回信息 | | |
| data |  |  |  | 执行结果: 返回查询的药品库存数据 | | |
| id | data | string |  | 库存id | | |

| drug\_id | data | string |  | 药品id | | |
| lot | data | string |  | 批次 | | |
| lot\_no | data | string |  | 批号 | | |
| supplier\_id | data | string |  | 供应商id | | |
| manufacturer | data | string |  | 生产商 | | |
| sourceland | data | string |  | 原产地 | | |
| approval\_no | data | string |  | 批准文号 | | |
| expiry\_date | data | date |  | 效期 | | |
| occupay\_qty | data | number |  | 占用数量 | | |
| actual\_qty | data | number |  | 实际数量 | | |
| actual\_cost | data | number |  | 实际成本 | | |
| actual\_charge | data | number |  | 实际金额 | | |
| actual\_spread | data | number |  | 实际差价 | | |
| purchase\_cost | data | number |  | 上次采购价 | | |
| price | data | number |  | 上次零售价 | | |
| production\_date | data | string |  | 生产日期 | | |
| storehouse | data | string |  | 库房名称 | | |
| is\_stop | data | int |  | 是否停用 | | |
| business\_price | data | number |  | 采购单位零售价(未用) | | |
| business\_cost\_price | data | number |  | 采购单位成本价(未用) | | |
| purchase\_cost\_price | data | number |  | 采购单位成本价（基层使用） | | |
| purchase\_price | data | number |  | 采购单位零售价（基层使用） | | |
| bar\_code | data | string |  | 追溯条码:主要用于记录高值耗材追溯条码 | | |
| is\_virtual | data | int |  | 虚拟库存标记:1-代表虚拟标记 | | |
| name | data | string |  | 药品通用名称 | | |

| brand\_name | data | string |  | 药品商品名称 | | |

## 2.6H1005查询药品申领记录

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **H1005** | | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **H1005查询药品申领记录（V1.0）** | | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/drug/DrugApply/GetDrugApply** | | | | | |
| **功能简述** | **药品申领单记录** | | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | | |
| 1、药品申领单记录。  2、适用于三方系统进行药品申领单记录 | | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "org\_id": "string",  "storehouse\_id": "string",  "s\_create\_time": "",  "e\_create\_time": "",  "s\_audit\_time": "",  "e\_audit\_time": "",  "creator": "",  "auditor": "",  "no\_sign": 0,  "no": "",  "drug\_id": "",  "is\_audit": 0,  "not\_audit": 0,  "page\_num": 0,  "page\_size": 0,  "is\_strike": 0,  "product\_id": ""  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| storehouse\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 申领部门id（B1002服务返回的id字段） |
| s\_create\_time |  | string |  | |  | 填制开始日期 |
| e\_create\_time |  | string |  | |  | 填制结束日期 |
| s\_audit\_time |  | string |  | |  | 审核开始日期 |
| e\_audit\_time |  | string |  | |  | 审核结束日期 |
| creator |  | string |  | |  | 填制人名称 |
| auditor |  | string |  | |  | 审核人名称 |
| no\_sign |  | int |  | |  | 单据标志(是否传入单据号(no)条件标志)，1：表示传入单据号，0：表示不传入单据号 |
| no |  | string |  | |  | 单据号，no\_sign=1该条件生效 |
| drug\_id |  | string |  | |  | 药品id |
| is\_audit |  | int |  | |  | 已审核，配合审核时间使用，若输入了审核开始结束时间，该参数传1，否则传0 |
| not\_audit |  | int |  | |  | 未审核，配合填制时间使用，若输入了填制开始结束时间，该参数传1，否则传0 |
| page\_num |  | int | **√** | |  | 当前第几页 |
| page\_size |  | int | **√** | |  | 一页多少条数据 |
| is\_strike |  | int |  | |  | 是否冲销，1：选择后查询冲销负记录，0：不显示冲销负记录 |
| product\_id |  | string |  | |  | 产品id |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |

## 2.10H1009药品领用单记录

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | | |
| 1、药品领用单记录。  2、适用于三方系统进行药品领用单记录 | | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "org\_id": "string",  "storehouse\_id": "string",  "no": "string",  "not\_audit": 0,  "s\_create\_time": "",  "e\_create\_time": "",  "is\_audit": 0,  "s\_audit\_time": "",  "e\_audit\_time": "",  "writeoff": 0,  "creator": "string",  "auditor": "string",  "drug\_id": "string",  "other\_dept\_id": "string",  "page\_num": 0,  "page\_size": 0,  "product\_id": "string"  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| storehouse\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 库房id，发药部门id |
| no |  | string |  | |  | 单据号 |
| not\_audit |  | int |  | |  | 未审核，配合填制时间使用，若输入了填制开始结束时间，该参数传1，否则传0 |
| s\_create\_time |  | string |  | |  | 填制开始日期 |
| e\_create\_time |  | string |  | |  | 填制结束日期 |
| is\_audit |  | int |  | |  | 已审核，配合审核时间使用，若输入了审核开始结束时间，该参数传1，否则传0 |
| s\_audit\_time |  | string |  | |  | 审核开始日期 |
| e\_audit\_time |  | string |  | |  | 审核结束日期 |
| writeoff |  | int |  | |  | 是否冲销（是否查询冲销负记录），1：是，0：否 |
| creator |  | string |  | |  | 填制人名称 |
| auditor |  | string |  | |  | 审核人名称 |
| drug\_id |  | string |  | |  | 药品id |
| other\_dept\_id |  | string |  | |  | 领用科室ID |
| page\_num |  | int | **√** | |  | 当前第几页 |
| page\_size |  | int | **√** | |  | 一页多少条数据 |
| product\_id |  | int |  | |  | 产品id |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "code": 200,  "msg": "查询成功!",  "data": {  "sum": {  "cost\_gap": 0,  "price\_charge": 12,  "cost": 12,  "spread": 0  },  "Total": 2,  "PageList": [  {  "id": "5606138970510922986",  "no": "2309000002",  "other\_dept": "住院内科",  "cost": 10,  "price\_charge": 10,  "spread": 0,  "creator": "管理员",  "create\_time": "2023-09-19 16:30:18",  "auditor": "",  "audit\_time": null,  "rec\_status": 0,  "description": "【原申领单号：2309000004】",  "audit\_suggestion": "",  "other\_dept\_id": "ddaee6a44fd6e5fc",  "bill\_sign": 0,  "apply\_id": "5667601150170354218",  "charge\_against": "",  "recipient": "七七1",  "status": 0  }  ]  },  "timestamp": 1695091416,  "innermsg": ""  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **数组** | **说明** | | |
| code |  | int |  | 返回结果: 200-成功; 500-失败 | | |
| msg |  | string |  | 返回信息 | | |
| data |  |  |  | 执行结果 | | |
| Total | data | int |  | 查询数据总数 | | |
| sum | data |  |  | 合计信息 | | |
| cost\_gap | sum | number |  | 成本金额差合计（未使用） | | |
| price\_charge | sum | number |  | 零售金额合计 | | |
| cost | sum | number |  | 成本金额合计 | | |
| spread | sum | number |  | 差价金额合计 | | |
| PageList | data |  |  | 查询数据信息 | | |

## 2.13H1012药品领用单冲销单据查询

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **H1012** | | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **H1012药品领用单冲销单据查询（V1.0）** | | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/drug/DrugBillStrikes/GetDrugStrikes** | | | | | |
| **功能简述** | **药品领用单冲销单据查询** | | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | | |
| 1、药品领用单冲销单据查询。  2、适用于三方系统进行药品领用单冲销单据查询 | | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "id":"",  "org\_id":"",  "category":0,  "show\_unit":"1"  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| id |  | string | **√** | |  | 领用记录id（H1009返回的领用记录id），入库退库冲销查询则该字段为入库记录id（H1019返回的入库记录id），移库冲销查询则该字段为移出库房记录id（H1035服务返回的移出记录id） |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| category |  | int | **√** | |  | 类别：0-非中草药;1-中草药 (根据部门性质来判断是否是中草药和非中草药,有中药房中药库性质的部门传入1;反之传入 0:默认为0 |
| show\_unit |  | int | **√** | |  | 显示单位：0-采购单位;1-售价单位默认为1 |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |

| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **数组** | **说明** | | |
| code |  | int |  | 返回结果: 200-成功; 500-失败 | | |
| msg |  | string |  | 返回信息 | | |
| data |  |  |  | 执行结果 | | |

| is\_external |  | int |  | |  | 是否向外部申领:0-否;1-是 |
| is\_show\_unit |  | int | **√** | |  | 显示单位，1：售价单位，0：药库单位 |

## 3.1H1015药品外购入库入库药品查询

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **H1015** | | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **H1015药品外购入库入库药品查询 （V1.0）** | | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/drug/drugDrugInfo/GetDrugByStorehouseId** | | | | | |
| **功能简述** | **查询药品外购入库入库药品** | | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | | |
| 1、查询药品外购入库药品信息。  2、适用于三方系统进行查询药品外购入库药品信息 | | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "keyword":"",  "org\_id":"",  "storehouse\_id":"",  "business\_unit":"0",  "product\_id":""  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| keyword |  | string | **√** | |  | 关键字，根据药品名称或编码检索药品 |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| storehouse\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 库房id |
| business\_unit |  | string | **√** | |  | 药品单位，1：售价单位，0：药库单位 |
| product\_id |  | string |  | |  | 产品id |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "code": 200,  "msg": "获取药品信息列表成功",  "data": [  {  "id": "979d1fcc250632e9",  "code": "040201",  "country\_code": "H32102547812",  "country\_norm\_name": "",  "platform\_code": "",  "platform\_name": "",  "category": "6",  "essential\_drugs\_code": "",  "name": "三九感冒颗粒",  "strength": "10g\*10袋/盒",  "manufacturer": "安徽安科",  "sourceland": "",  "lot": "",  "lot\_no": "",  "max\_expiry": 0,  "approval\_no": "",  "register\_no": "",  "unit": "盒",  "purchase\_cost": 2,  "price": 3,  "limit\_price": 0,  "is\_storehouse\_batch": "否",  "is\_pharmacy\_batch": "否",  "is\_change": "是",  "is\_public": "共用",  "py\_code": "SJGMKL,DVDJJO",  "qty": 29,  "is\_apply\_other\_org\_stock": 1,  "max": 0,  "min": 0,  "add\_rate": 0,  "supplier\_id": "7b88b57fcb77a501",  "supplier\_name": "东拉西扯"  }  ]  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **数组** | **说明** | | |
| code |  | int |  | 返回结果: 200-成功; 500-失败 | | |
| msg |  | string |  | 返回信息 | | |
| data |  |  |  | 执行结果: 返回查询的药品数据 | | |
| id | data | string |  | 药品id | | |
| code | data | string |  | 编码 | | |
| country\_code | data | string |  | 国家编码 | | |
| country\_norm\_name | data | string |  | 国家惯标名称 | | |

| platform\_name | data | string |  | 平台名称 | | |
| category | data | string |  | 类别：4-卫材;5-西药;6-中成药;7-中草药 | | |

| strength | data | string |  | 规格 | | |
| manufacturer | data | string |  | 生产商 | | |
| sourceland | data | string |  | 原产地 | | |

| register\_no | data | string |  | 注册证号 | | |
| unit | data | string |  | 售价单位 | | |
| purchase\_cost | data | number |  | 成本价 | | |
| price | data | number |  | 零售价 | | |
| limit\_price | data | number |  | 采购限价 | | |

| qty | data | number |  | 当前库存的数量(用于参考) | | |

| max | data | number |  | 上限 | | |
| min | data | number |  | 下限 | | |
| add\_rate | data | number |  | 加成率 | | |

## 3.5H1019药品外购入库记录

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **H1019** | | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **H1019药品外购入库记录（V1.0）** | | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/drug/DrugBuyIn/GetDrugInIo** | | | | | |
| **功能简述** | **查询药品外购入库记录记录** | | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | | |
| 1、药品外购入库记录。  2、适用于三方系统进行查询药品外购入库记录 | | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "org\_id": "string",  "storehouse\_id": "string",  "s\_create\_time": "",  "e\_create\_time": "",  "s\_audit\_time": "",  "e\_audit\_time": "",  "creator": "",  "auditor": "",  "no\_sign": 0,  "no": "",  "drug\_id": "",  "is\_audit": 0,  "not\_audit": 0,  "page\_num": 0,  "page\_size": 0,  "is\_strike": 0,  "product\_id": ""  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| storehouse\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 库房id |
| s\_create\_time |  | string |  | |  | 填制开始日期 |
| e\_create\_time |  | string |  | |  | 填制结束日期 |
| s\_audit\_time |  | string |  | |  | 审核开始日期 |
| e\_audit\_time |  | string |  | |  | 审核结束日期 |
| creator |  | string |  | |  | 填制人名称 |
| auditor |  | string |  | |  | 审核人名称 |
| no\_sign |  | int |  | |  | 单据标志(是否传入单据号(no)条件标志)，1：表示传入单据号，0：表示不传入单据号 |
| no |  | string |  | |  | 单据号，no\_sign=1该条件生效 |
| drug\_id |  | string |  | |  | 药品id |
| is\_audit |  | int |  | |  | 已审核，配合审核时间使用，若输入了审核开始结束时间，该参数传1，否则传0 |
| not\_audit |  | int |  | |  | 未审核，配合填制时间使用，若输入了填制开始结束时间，该参数传1，否则传0 |
| page\_num |  | int | **√** | |  | 当前第几页 |
| page\_size |  | int | **√** | |  | 一页多少条数据 |

| product\_id |  | string |  | |  | 产品id |
| supplier\_id |  | string |  | |  | 供应商id |
| category |  | int | **√** | |  | 类别：0-非中草药;1-中草药 (根据部门性质来判断是否是中草药和非中草药,有中药房中药库性质的部门传入1;反之传入 0:默认为0 |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "code": 200,  "msg": "查询成功!",  "data": {  "sum": {  "cost\_gap": 0,  "price\_charge": 2,  "cost": 2,  "spread": 0  },  "Total": 1,  "PageList": [  {  "id": "4922667338506204270",  "no": "2309000001",  "other\_dept": "住院内科",  "cost": 2,  "price\_charge": 2,  "spread": 0,  "creator": "管理员",  "create\_time": "2023-09-19 16:15:32",  "auditor": "",  "audit\_time": null,  "rec\_status": 0,  "description": "【原申领单号：2309000003】",  "audit\_suggestion": "",  "other\_dept\_id": "ddaee6a44fd6e5fc",  "bill\_sign": 0,  "apply\_id": "5233451538145882856",  "charge\_against": "",  "recipient": "七七1",  "status": 0  }  ]  },  "timestamp": 1695263158,  "innermsg": ""  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **数组** | **说明** | | |

# 药品移库数据接口详情示例

## 4.1H1028药品移库单新增提交

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **H1028** | | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **H1028药品移库单新增提交（V1.0）** | | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/drug/DrugShift/AddDrugShift** | | | | | |
| **功能简述** | **药品移库单新增提交** | | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | | |
| 1、药品移库单新增提交。  2、适用于三方系统进行药品移库单新增提交 | | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "org\_id": "string",  "no": "string",  "other\_org\_id": "string",  "other\_org\_name": "string",  "storehouse\_id": "string",  "storehouse": "string",  "other\_dept\_id": "string",  "bill\_type": 201,  "other\_dept": "string",  "creator": "string",  "apply\_id": 0,  "show\_unit": 0,  "category": 0,  "description": "string",  "list\_detail": [  {  "sno": 0,  "drug\_id": "string",  "lot\_no": "string",  "lot": "string",  "approval\_no": "string",  "manufacturer": "string",  "supplier\_id": "string",  "production\_date": "2023-09-21T08:27:13.948Z",  "expiry\_date": "2023-09-21T08:27:13.948Z",  "qty": 0,  "actual\_qty": 0,  "unit": "string",  "business\_unit": "string",  "cost\_price": 0,  "cost": 0,  "price": 0,  "price\_charge": 0,  "spread": 0,  "business\_qty": 0,  "business\_cost\_price": 0,  "business\_price": 0,  "apply\_detail\_id": 0  }  ]  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| no |  | string |  | |  | 单据号,新增不填，传空，修改时必传（H1033服务返回的单据号no） |
| other\_org\_id |  | string |  | |  | 调入机构id 调拨时必填,移库时为空 |
| other\_org\_name |  | string |  | |  | 调入机构名称 外部调拨时必填,其他可选填 |
| storehouse\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 移出库房ID |
| storehouse |  | string | **√** | |  | 移出库房名称 |
| other\_dept\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 移入库房ID |
| other\_dept |  | string | **√** | |  | 移入库房名称 |
| bill\_type |  | string | **√** | |  | 单据类型：传304 |
| creator |  | string | **√** | |  | 填制人名称 |
| apply\_id |  | string |  | |  | 申领id(申领单转调拨单据时不允许为空,直接新增调拨单据时为空) |
| show\_unit |  | int | **√** | |  | 显示单位，1：售价单位，0：药库单位默认1 |
| category |  | int | **√** | |  | 类别：0-非中草药;1-中草药 (根据部门性质来判断是否是中草药和非中草药,有中药房中药库性质的部门传入1;反之传入 0:默认为0 |
| description |  | string |  | |  | 摘要 |
| list\_detail |  | string |  | |  | 单据明细 |
| sno | list\_detail | int | **√** | |  | 序号 |
| drug\_id | list\_detail | string | **√** | |  | 药品id |
| lot\_no | list\_detail | string | **√** | |  | 批号 |
| lot | list\_detail | string | **√** | |  | 批次 |
| approval\_no | list\_detail | string |  | |  | 批准文号 |
| manufacturer | list\_detail | string |  | |  | 生产商 |
| supplier\_id | list\_detail | string |  | |  | 供应商id |
| production\_date | list\_detail | string |  | |  | 生产日期 |
| expiry\_date | list\_detail | string |  | |  | 效期 |
| qty | list\_detail | number | **√** | |  | 填写数量 |
| actual\_qty | list\_detail | number |  | |  | 实际数量 |
| unit | list\_detail | string | **√** | |  | 单位 |
| business\_unit | list\_detail | string |  | |  | 业务单位 |
| cost\_price | list\_detail | number | **√** | |  | 成本价 |
| cost | list\_detail | number | **√** | |  | 成本金额 |
| price | list\_detail | number | **√** | |  | 零售价 |
| price\_charge | list\_detail | number | **√** | |  | 零售金额 |
| spread | list\_detail | number | **√** | |  | 差价 |
| business\_qty | list\_detail | number |  | |  | 业务单位数量 |
| business\_cost\_price | list\_detail | number |  | |  | 采购单位成本价 |
| business\_price | list\_detail | number |  | |  | 采购单位零售价 |
| apply\_detail\_id | list\_detail | string |  | |  | 明细id:直接新增调拨单据时传空,申领转调拨单据时必填 |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "code": 200,  "msg": "2309000003",  "data": "2309000003",  "timestamp": 1695285160,  "innermsg": ""  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **数组** | **说明** | | |
| code |  | int |  | 返回结果: 200-成功; 500-失败 | | |
| msg |  | string |  | 返回信息 | | |
| data |  |  |  | 执行结果: 返回单据号 | | |

## 4.4H1031药品移库取消

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "org\_id": "string",  "storehouse\_id": "string",  "no": "string",  "not\_audit": 0,  "s\_create\_time": "2023-09-22T01:12:47.802Z",  "e\_create\_time": "2023-09-22T01:12:47.802Z",  "is\_audit": 0,  "s\_audit\_time": "2023-09-22T01:12:47.802Z",  "e\_audit\_time": "2023-09-22T01:12:47.802Z",  "writeoff": 0,  "creator": "string",  "auditor": "string",  "drug\_id": "string",  "supplier\_id": "string",  "page\_num": 0,  "page\_size": 0,  "product\_id": "string"  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| storehouse\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 库房id（移出库房id） |
| no |  | string |  | |  | 单据号 |
| not\_audit |  | int |  | |  | 未审核，配合填制时间使用，若输入了填制开始结束时间，该参数传1，否则传0 |
| s\_create\_time |  | string |  | |  | 填制开始日期 |
| e\_create\_time |  | string |  | |  | 填制结束日期 |
| is\_audit |  | int |  | |  | 已审核，配合审核时间使用，若输入了审核开始结束时间，该参数传1，否则传0 |
| s\_audit\_time |  | string |  | |  | 审核开始日期 |
| e\_audit\_time |  | string |  | |  | 审核结束日期 |
| writeoff |  | int |  | |  | 是否冲销，1：选择后查询冲销负记录，0：不显示冲销负记录 |
| creator |  | string |  | |  | 填制人名称 |
| auditor |  | string |  | |  | 审核人名称 |
| drug\_id |  | string |  | |  | 药品id |
| supplier\_id |  | string |  | |  | 供应商id |
| page\_num |  | int | **√** | |  | 当前第几页 |
| page\_size |  | int | **√** | |  | 一页多少条数据 |
| product\_id |  | string |  | |  | 产品id |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "code": 200,  "msg": "",  "data": {  "sum": {  "cost\_gap": 0,  "price\_charge": 22,  "cost": 22,  "spread": 0  },  "Total": 2,  "PageList": [  {  "id": "5561016985007139990",  "no": "2309000004",  "shift\_storehouse": "西药库",  "cost": 2,  "price\_charge": 2,  "spread": 0,  "creator": "管理员",  "create\_time": "2023-09-22 09:08:41",  "receiver": "管理员",  "receive\_time": "2023-09-22 09:09:32",  "drug\_preparer": "",  "send\_time": null,  "rec\_status": 0,  "description": "",  "audit\_suggestion": "",  "shift\_storehouse\_id": "474a4fca4643f3b4",  "bill\_sign": 0,  "apply\_id": "0",  "reversal\_mark": "",  "bill\_type": "",  "status": 1  }  ]  },  "timestamp": 1695346161,  "innermsg": ""  } | | | | | | |

| msg |  | string |  | 返回信息 | | |

| sum | data |  |  | 合计信息 | | |
| cost\_gap | sum | number |  | 成本金额差合计（未使用） | | |

| cost | sum | number |  | 成本金额合计 | | |
| spread | sum | number |  | 差价金额合计 | | |

## 4.10H1039申领单转移库保存

| {  "org\_id": "string",  "no": "string",  "other\_org\_id": "string",  "other\_org\_name": "string",  "storehouse\_id": "string",  "storehouse": "string",  "other\_dept\_id": "string",  "bill\_type": 201,  "other\_dept": "string",  "creator": "string",  "apply\_id": 0,  "show\_unit": 0,  "category": 0,  "description": "string",  "list\_detail": [  {  "sno": 0,  "drug\_id": "string",  "lot\_no": "string",  "lot": "string",  "approval\_no": "string",  "manufacturer": "string",  "supplier\_id": "string",  "production\_date": "",  "expiry\_date": "",  "qty": 0,  "actual\_qty": 0,  "unit": "string",  "business\_unit": "string",  "cost\_price": 0,  "cost": 0,  "price": 0,  "price\_charge": 0,  "spread": 0,  "business\_qty": 0,  "business\_cost\_price": 0,  "business\_price": 0,  "apply\_detail\_id": 0  }  ]  } | | | | | | |

| {     **"org\_id"**: **"string"**,     **"class\_info"**: {         **"parent\_id"**: **""**,         **"code"**: **""**,         **"name"**: **""**,         **"py\_code"**: **""**     },     **"matl\_info"**: {         **"code"**: **"string"**,         **"is\_public"**: **0**,         **"is\_share"**: **0**,         **"name"**: **"string"**,         **"py\_code"**: **"string"**,         **"wb\_code"**: **"string"**,         **"strength"**: **"string"**,         **"max\_expiry"**: **0**,         **"unit"**: **"string"**,         **"packg\_unit"**: **"string"**,         **"unit\_coefficient"**: **0**,         **"price"**: **0**,         **"manufacturer"**: **"string"**,         **"platform\_code"**: **"string"**,         **"platform\_name"**: **"string"**,         **"description"**: **"string"**,         **"creator"**: **"string"**,         **"status"**: **0**     } } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| class\_info |  |  |  | | **√** | 分类信息 |
| matl\_info |  |  |  | | **√** | 物资目录信息 |

| code | class\_info | string |  | |  | 分类编码 |
| name | class\_info | string |  | | **√** | 分类名称，无分类会新增，有会获取分类id |
| py\_code | class\_info | string |  | |  | 分类简码 |
| code | matl\_info | string |  | |  | 目录编码 |
| is\_public | matl\_info | int |  | |  | 是否共用 |
| is\_share | matl\_info | int |  | |  | 是否适用所有机构 |
| name | matl\_info | string |  | |  | 目录名称 |
| py\_code | matl\_info | string |  | |  | 目录拼音码 |
| wb\_code | matl\_info | string |  | |  | 目录五笔码 |
| strength | matl\_info | string |  | |  | 规格 |
| max\_expiry | matl\_info | int |  | |  | 最大效期 |
| unit | matl\_info | string |  | |  | 单位 |
| packg\_unit | matl\_info | string |  | |  | 包装单位 |
| unit\_coefficient | matl\_info | int |  | |  | 单位系数 |
| price | matl\_info | number |  | |  | 单价 |
| manufacturer | matl\_info | string |  | |  | 生产商 |

| creator | matl\_info | string |  | |  | 创建人 |
| status | matl\_info | string |  | |  | 状态，1-审核；0-未审核 |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |
| {     **"code"**: **200**,     **"msg"**: **"新增成功"**,     **"data"**: **"8ae528a386a984f6"**,     **"timestamp"**: **1711521512**,     **"innermsg"**: **""** } | | | | | | |

## W2001A新增物资采购入库单据

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **W2001A** | | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **W2001A新增物资采购入库单据（V1.0）** | | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/AddMatlByIn** | | | | | |
| **功能简述** | **新增物资采购入库单据** | | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | | |
| 1、新增物资采购入库单据 | | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {     **"org\_id"**: **"string"**,     **"storehouse\_id"**: **"string"**,     **"storehouse"**: **"string"**,     **"is\_show\_unit"**: **0**,     **"supplier\_id"**: **"string"**,     **"invoice\_no"**: **"string"**,     **"description"**: **"string"**,     **"creator"**: **"string"**,     **"creator\_id"**: **"string"**,     **"total\_charge"**: **0**,     **"is\_batches"**: **0**,     **"no"**: **"string"**,     **"list\_detail"**: [         {             **"matl\_id"**: **"string"**,             **"code"**: **"string"**,             **"manufacturer"**: **"string"**,             **"manufacturer\_code"**: **"string"**,             **"lot\_no"**: **"string"**,             **"production\_date"**: **"2024-03-27T02:40:08.711Z"**,             **"expiry\_date"**: **"2024-03-27T02:40:08.711Z"**,             **"unit"**: **"string"**,             **"qty"**: **0**,             **"price"**: **0**,             **"charge"**: **0**,             **"apply\_no"**: **"string"**,             **"name"**: **"string"**,             **"is\_external"**: **0**         }     ] } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| storehouse\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 库房id |
| storehouse |  | string | **√** | |  | 库房名称 |
| is\_show\_unit |  | int | **√** | |  | 显示单位；1-单位；0-包装单位 |
| supplier\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 供应商id |
| invoice\_no |  | string |  | |  | 发票号 |
| description |  | string |  | |  | 说明 |
| creator |  | string | **√** | |  | 创建人 |
| creator\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 创建人id |
| total\_charge |  | string | **√** | |  | 合计 |
| is\_batches |  | int | **√** | |  | 物资库房是否分批管理，1-分批；0-不分批 |
| no |  | string |  | |  | 单据号；不传系统默认生成我们系统的单据号 |
| list\_detail |  |  | **√** | | **√** | 单据明细 |
| matl\_id | list\_detail | string | **√** | |  | 物资目录id，新增目录时的id传入 |
| code | list\_detail | string | **√** | |  | 物资编码 |
| manufacturer | list\_detail | string |  | |  | 物资生产商 |
| lot\_no | list\_detail | string |  | |  | 批号 |
| production\_date | list\_detail | string | **√** | |  | 生产日期 |
| expiry\_date | list\_detail | string | **√** | |  | 效期 |
| unit | list\_detail | string | **√** | |  | 单位 |
| qty | list\_detail | number | **√** | |  | 数量 |
| price | list\_detail | number | **√** | |  | 单价 |
| charge | list\_detail | number | **√** | |  | 单价合计；数量\*单位 |
| name | list\_detail | string |  | |  | 物资名称 |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |
| {     **"code"**: **200**,     **"msg"**: **"新增成功"**,     **"data"**: **"2403000004"**,     **"timestamp"**: **1711524154**,     **"innermsg"**: **""** } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **数组** | **说明** | | |

| msg |  | string |  | 返回信息 | | |

| class\_id |  | string | **√** |  | 分类id |

| {     **"code"**: **200**,     **"msg"**: **"更新成功"**,     **"data"**: **null**,     **"timestamp"**: **1711521856**,     **"innermsg"**: **""** } | | | | | |

| footnote | drug\_details | string |  |  | 脚注 |
| category | drug\_details | int |  |  | 药品类别 4-卫材;5-西药;6-中成药;7-中草药 |
| is\_trace | drug\_details | int |  |  | 跟踪在用 卫材传入是否跟踪再用属性,药品类的默认传入1 |
| exec\_class | drug\_details | int |  |  | 给药途径分类：0-未明确,1-输液类,2-注射类;3-口服类，仅给药途径使用 |
| prop | drug\_details | int |  |  | 医嘱效期：0-临嘱；1-长嘱 |
| give\_mode | drug\_details | int |  |  | 发药方式：4-正常 5-外购药 6-自备药(外) 7-离院带药 8-自取药 9-自备药（内） 10-不计费 11-分组药 |
| bar\_code | drug\_details | string |  |  | 追溯条码:主要用于记录高值耗材追溯条码 |
| give\_source\_code | drug\_details | int |  |  | 1：门诊，2：住院 |
| **出参示例** | | | | | |
| {  "code": 200,  "msg": "",  "data": "2310000022",  "timestamp": 1698033410,  "innermsg": ""  } | | | | | |

| msg |  | string |  | 返回信息 | |

| anti\_type | variety\_info | int |  |  | 抗菌药物：1-非限制使用；2-限制使用；3-特殊使用 |

| status | variety\_info | int |  |  | 0-未审核;1正常;-1停用（传1） |
| create\_org\_id | variety\_info | string | **√** |  | 创建机构id |
| is\_prescription | variety\_info | int |  |  | 是否处方用药:0-非处方用药,1-处方用药 |
| is\_share | variety\_info | int | **√** |  | is\_share:是否共用 1-是;0-否 |
| is\_all\_org | variety\_info | int | **√** |  | 是否适用于所有机构 1-是;0-否 |
| tcm\_type | variety\_info | int |  |  | 型态标识：0-普通;1-制剂;2-协定药;3-免煎饮片;4-包装饮片 |
| purchase\_unit | variety\_info | string | **√** |  | 采购单位（同drug\_info中的purchase\_unit一致） |
| unit | variety\_info | string | **√** |  | 售价单位（同drug\_info中的purchase\_unit一致） |
| dosage\_coefficient | variety\_info | number | **√** |  | 剂量系数（用于规格售价单位显示） |
| purchase\_unit\_base | variety\_info | int | **√** |  | 采购包装基数（同drug\_info中的purchase\_unit\_base一致） |
| purchase\_unit\_coefficient | variety\_info | int | **√** |  | 采购单位系数（同drug\_info中的purchase\_unit\_coefficient一致） |
| is\_change | variety\_info | int | **√** |  | 是否变价 1-是（时价）;0-否（定价） |
| limit\_price | variety\_info | number |  |  | 采购限价 |

## **12.2H1048获取收入科目**

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **H1048** | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **H1048获取收入科目（V1.0）** | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/fee/FeeItem/GetIncomeItemDown** | | | | |
| **功能简述** | **获取收入科目** | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | |
| 1、获取收入科目。  2、适用于三方系统进行收入科目查询 | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | |
| {  "org\_id":"" ,  "prop": 0  } | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | **数组** | **说明** |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** |  | 机构id |
| prop |  | string | **√** |  | 1-收费项目调用;2-药品调用:0-查询所有,不分药品收费,这里传2 |
| **出参示例** | | | | | |
| {  "code": 200,  "msg": "执行完成",  "data": [  {  "id": "1",  "name": "药品收入",  "income\_item\_list": [  {  "id": "f222a8289b2d333",  "name": "耗材费",  "item\_type": 1,  "py\_code": "HCF"  },  {  "id": "101",  "name": "西药费",  "item\_type": 1,  "py\_code": "XYF"  },  {  "id": "102",  "name": "中成药",  "item\_type": 1,  "py\_code": "ZCY"  },  {  "id": "103",  "name": "中草药",  "item\_type": 1,  "py\_code": "ZCY"  }  ]  }  ],  "timestamp": 1701684067,  "innermsg": ""  } | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **数组** | **说明** | |
| code |  | int |  | 返回结果: 200-成功; 500-失败 | |
| msg |  | string |  | 返回信息 | |
| data |  |  |  | 返回数据 | |
| id | data | string |  | 收入科目分类id | |
| name | data | string |  | 收入科目分类名称 | |
| income\_item\_list | data |  |  | 收入科目列表 | |
| id | income\_item\_list | string |  | 收入科目id | |
| name | income\_item\_list | string |  | 收入科目名称 | |
| item\_type | income\_item\_list | int |  | 项目类型：0-分类；1-明细 | |
| py\_code | income\_item\_list | string |  | 简码 | |

## **12.6 H1085A药品/卫材调成本价**

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **H1085A** | | | | |

| **功能简述** | **获取药品分类信息** | | | | |

## **12.7 H1085B药品/卫材调售价**

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **H1085B** | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **H1085B药品/卫材调售价（V1.0）** | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/drug/DrugClass/DrugAdjustCostPrice** | | | | |
| **功能简述** | **获取药品分类信息** | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | |
| 1. 用售价单位进行调价 2. 支持调库存价 | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | |
| {     **"id"**: **"string"**,     **"change"**: **0**,     **"is\_change"**: **0**,     **"drug\_id"**: **"string"**,     **"org\_id"**: **"string"**,     **"history\_price"**: **0**,     **"now\_price"**: **0**,     **"history\_cost\_price"**: **0**,     **"cost\_price"**: **0**,     **"income\_item\_id"**: **"string"**,     **"adjuster"**: **"string"**,     **"description"**: **"string"**,     **"exec\_time"**: **"2026-01-20T08:58:24.197Z"**,     **"exec\_moment"**: **0**,     **"show\_unit"**: **"string"**,     **"adjust\_id"**: **0**,     **"drug\_stock"**: [         {             **"org\_id"**: **"string"**,             **"storehouse\_id"**: **"string"**,             **"storehouse"**: **"string"**,             **"drug\_id"**: **"string"**,             **"name"**: **"string"**,             **"strength"**: **"string"**,             **"unit"**: **"string"**,             **"is\_change"**: **0**,             **"lot\_no"**: **"string"**,             **"actual\_qty"**: **0**,             **"lot"**: **"string"**,             **"history\_price"**: **0**,             **"price"**: **0**,             **"history\_cost\_price"**: **0**,             **"cost\_price"**: **0**,             **"expiry\_date"**: **"2026-01-20T08:58:24.197Z"**,             **"manufacturer"**: **"string"**,             **"supplier"**: **"string"**,             **"supplier\_id"**: **"string"**,             **"purchase\_price\_sum"**: **0**,             **"purchase\_cost\_price\_sum"**: **0**         }     ] } | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | **数组** | **说明** |
| id |  | string | **√** |  | 收费价目id |
| change |  | int |  |  |  |
| is\_change |  | int |  |  | 是否变价 |
| drug\_id |  | string | **√** |  | 药品规格id |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** |  | 机构id |
| history\_price |  | number | **√** |  | 原价 |
| now\_price |  | number | **√** |  | 现售价 |
| history\_cost\_price |  | number | **√** |  | 原成本价 |
| cost\_price |  | number | **√** |  | 现成本价 |
| income\_item\_id |  | string |  |  |  |
| adjuster |  | string | **√** |  | 调价人 |
| description |  | string |  |  | 说明 |
| exec\_time |  | DateTime | **√** |  | 执行时间 |
| exec\_moment |  | int |  |  | 1-立即执行;0-未来价 |
| drug\_stock |  |  |  | **√** | 库存信息 |
| org\_id | drug\_stock | string |  |  | 机构id |
| storehouse\_id | drug\_stock | string |  |  | 库房id |
| storehouse | drug\_stock | string |  |  | 库房名称 |
| drug\_id | drug\_stock | string |  |  | 规格id |
| name | drug\_stock | string |  |  | 名称 |
| strength | drug\_stock | string |  |  | 规格 |
| unit | drug\_stock | string |  |  | 单位 |
| is\_change | drug\_stock | int |  |  | 是否变价 |

| actual\_qty | drug\_stock | number |  |  | 实际数量 |
| lot | drug\_stock | long |  |  | 批次 |
| history\_price | drug\_stock | number |  |  | 原售价 |
| price | drug\_stock | number |  |  | 现售价 |
| history\_cost\_price | drug\_stock | number |  |  | 原成本价 |
| cost\_price | drug\_stock | number |  |  | 现成本价 |
| expiry\_date | drug\_stock | string |  |  | 效期 |
| manufacturer | drug\_stock | string |  |  | 生厂商（名称） |
| supplier | drug\_stock | string |  |  | 供应商（名称） |
| supplier\_id | drug\_stock | string |  |  | 供应商id |
| **出参示例** | | | | | |

# 药品进销存数据接口详情示例

## A4001商品盘存上传

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **A4001** | | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **A4001商品盘存上传（V1.0）** | | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/drug/GetInventoryInfo** | | | | | |
| **功能简述** | **根据开始、结束时间及机构查询所有药品盘点数据信息** | | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | | |
| 1. 查询药品盘点信息。 2. 适用于三方系统进行新增盘点数据 | | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "org\_id": "",  "start\_time": "",  "end\_time": ""  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| start\_time |  | string | **√** | |  | 开始时间 |
| end\_time |  | string | **√** | |  | 结束时间 |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "code": "200",  "msg": "查询商品盘存上传信息成功！",  "data": [  {  "prod\_stoin\_id": "5013090517888055513",  "prod\_type": 1,  "med\_list\_codg": "280103",  "fixmedins\_hilist\_id": "zlsoft",  "fixmedins\_hilist\_name": "中联区卫",  "rx\_flag": "",  "invdate": "2023-08-21 11:28:11",  "ord\_no": "2308000002",  "inv\_cnt": 1,  "pric": 19,  "spler\_code": null,  "spler\_name": null,  "manu\_lotnum": "",  "batch\_number": "0",  "fixmedins\_bchno": "0(307-2308000002)",  "manu\_date": null,  "expy\_end": null,  "storageroomname": "测试药房",  "stockstatus": 1,  "memo": ""  }  ]  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **数组** | **说明** | | |
| code |  | int |  | 返回结果: 200-成功; 500-失败 | | |
| msg |  | string |  | 返回信息 | | |
| data |  |  |  | 执行结果: 返回查询的盘点信息数据 | | |
| prod\_stoin\_id | data | string |  | 商品入库记录主键, 院内惟一 | | |
| prod\_type | data | int |  | 商品类型1、药品2、耗材、3、器械 | | |
| med\_list\_codg | data | string |  | 医疗目录编码 | | |
| fixmedins\_hilist\_id | data | string |  | 定点医药机构目录编号 | | |
| fixmedins\_hilist\_name | data | string |  | 定点医药机构目录名称 | | |
| rx\_flag | data | string |  | 处方药标志 | | |
| invdate | data | string |  | 盘存日期 | | |
| ord\_no | data | string |  | 订单号,如在省公共资源交易中心采购-订单号，否则不用 | | |
| inv\_cnt | data | number |  | 库存数量,按最小计价包装单位统计 | | |
| pric | data | number |  | 单价 | | |
| spler\_code | data | string |  | 供应商编码,指配送企业编码 | | |
| spler\_name | data | string |  | 供应商名称,指配送企业名称 | | |
| manu\_lotnum | data | string |  | 生产批号 | | |
| batch\_number | data | string |  | 批次号,同品、同批用作销售的 | | |
| fixmedins\_bchno | data | string |  | 定点医药机构批次流水号,医药机构自定义批次号 | | |
| manu\_date | data | string |  | 生产日期 | | |
| expy\_end | data | string |  | 有效期止 | | |
| storageroomname | data | string |  | 库房名称 | | |
| stockstatus | data | int |  | 库存状态,库存状态，1 正常、2 缺货、3 停止挂网 | | |
| memo | data | string |  | 备注 | | |

## A4002商品库存变更

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **A4002** | | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **A4002商品库存变更（V1.0）** | | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/drug/GetStockChangeInfo** | | | | | |
| **功能简述** | **根据开始、结束时间及机构查询药品库存变更信息** | | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | | |
| 1、查询药品变更信息。  2、适用于三方系统进行新增药品变更数据 | | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "org\_id": "",  "start\_time": "",  "end\_time": ""  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| start\_time |  | string | **√** | |  | 开始时间 |
| end\_time |  | string | **√** | |  | 结束时间 |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "code": "200",  "msg": "查询商品库存变更信息成功！",  "data": [  {  "med\_list\_codg": "100000100801",  "inv\_chg\_type": "1",  "fixmedins\_hilist\_id": "zlsoft",  "fixmedins\_hilist\_name": "中联区卫",  "fixmedins\_bchno": "20230413170544001(1-2309000001)",  "pric": 11.5,  "cnt": 0,  "rx\_flag": "",  "inv\_chg\_time": "2023-09-01 03:02:04",  "inv\_chg\_opter\_name": "郑静",  "memo": "药品处方新增",  "trdn\_flag": "",  "prod\_stoin\_id": "4862936721226687822",  "inv\_cnt": 999884  }  ]  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **数组** | **说明** | | |
| code |  | int |  | 返回结果: 200-成功; 500-失败 | | |
| msg |  | string |  | 返回信息 | | |
| data |  |  |  | 执行结果: 返回查询的库存变更数据 | | |
| med\_list\_codg | data | string |  | 医疗目录编码 | | |
| inv\_chg\_type | data | string |  | 库存变更类型 | | |
| fixmedins\_hilist\_id | data | string |  | 定点医药机构目录编号 | | |
| fixmedins\_hilist\_name | data | string |  | 定点医药机构目录名称 | | |
| fixmedins\_bchno | data | string |  | 定点医药机构批次流水号 | | |
| pric | data | number |  | 单价 | | |
| cnt | data | number |  | 数量 | | |
| rx\_flag | data | string |  | 处方药标志 | | |
| inv\_chg\_time | data | string |  | 库存变更时间 | | |
| inv\_chg\_opter\_name | data | string |  | 库存变更经办人姓名 | | |
| memo | data | string |  | 备注 | | |

## 2.2H1001获取药品库存信息

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **H1001** | | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **H1001获取药品库存信息 （V1.0）** | | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/drug/GetDrugStockInfo** | | | | | |
| **功能简述** | **查询药品库存信息** | | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | | |
| 1、查询药品库存信息。  2、适用于三方系统进行查询药品库存信息 | | | | | | |

| keyword |  | String |  | |  | 关键字，根据药品名称或编码检索药品 |

| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **数组** | **说明** | | |
| code |  | int |  | 返回结果: 200-成功; 500-失败 | | |
| msg |  | string |  | 返回信息 | | |
| data |  |  |  | 执行结果: 返回查询的药品库存数据 | | |

| purchase\_cost\_price | data | number |  | 采购单位成本价（基层使用） | | |

| is\_virtual | data | int |  | 虚拟库存标记:1-代表虚拟标记 | | |
| name | data | string |  | 药品通用名称 | | |
| code | data | string |  | 药品编码 | | |
| brand\_name | data | string |  | 药品商品名称 | | |

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |

| **入参示例** | | | | | | |

| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |

| no |  | string |  | |  | 单据号，no\_sign=1该条件生效 |
| drug\_id |  | string |  | |  | 药品id |
| is\_audit |  | int |  | |  | 已审核，配合审核时间使用，若输入了审核开始结束时间，该参数传1，否则传0 |
| not\_audit |  | int |  | |  | 未审核，配合填制时间使用，若输入了填制开始结束时间，该参数传1，否则传0 |
| page\_num |  | int | **√** | |  | 当前第几页 |
| page\_size |  | int | **√** | |  | 一页多少条数据 |
| is\_strike |  | int |  | |  | 是否冲销，1：选择后查询冲销负记录，0：不显示冲销负记录 |
| product\_id |  | string |  | |  | 产品id |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |

| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **数组** | **说明** | | |

## 2.10H1009药品领用单记录

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | | |
| 1、药品领用单记录。  2、适用于三方系统进行药品领用单记录 | | | | | | |

| {  "org\_id": "string",  "storehouse\_id": "string",  "no": "string",  "not\_audit": 0,  "s\_create\_time": "",  "e\_create\_time": "",  "is\_audit": 0,  "s\_audit\_time": "",  "e\_audit\_time": "",  "writeoff": 0,  "creator": "string",  "auditor": "string",  "drug\_id": "string",  "other\_dept\_id": "string",  "page\_num": 0,  "page\_size": 0,  "product\_id": "string"  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |

| no |  | string |  | |  | 单据号 |
| not\_audit |  | int |  | |  | 未审核，配合填制时间使用，若输入了填制开始结束时间，该参数传1，否则传0 |
| s\_create\_time |  | string |  | |  | 填制开始日期 |
| e\_create\_time |  | string |  | |  | 填制结束日期 |
| is\_audit |  | int |  | |  | 已审核，配合审核时间使用，若输入了审核开始结束时间，该参数传1，否则传0 |
| s\_audit\_time |  | string |  | |  | 审核开始日期 |
| e\_audit\_time |  | string |  | |  | 审核结束日期 |
| writeoff |  | int |  | |  | 是否冲销（是否查询冲销负记录），1：是，0：否 |
| creator |  | string |  | |  | 填制人名称 |
| auditor |  | string |  | |  | 审核人名称 |
| drug\_id |  | string |  | |  | 药品id |
| other\_dept\_id |  | string |  | |  | 领用科室ID |
| page\_num |  | int | **√** | |  | 当前第几页 |
| page\_size |  | int | **√** | |  | 一页多少条数据 |
| product\_id |  | int |  | |  | 产品id |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |

| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **数组** | **说明** | | |

| data |  |  |  | 执行结果 | | |

## 2.13H1012药品领用单冲销单据查询

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **H1012** | | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **H1012药品领用单冲销单据查询（V1.0）** | | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/drug/DrugBillStrikes/GetDrugStrikes** | | | | | |
| **功能简述** | **药品领用单冲销单据查询** | | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | | |
| 1、药品领用单冲销单据查询。  2、适用于三方系统进行药品领用单冲销单据查询 | | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "id":"",  "org\_id":"",  "category":0,  "show\_unit":"1"  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| id |  | string | **√** | |  | 领用记录id（H1009返回的领用记录id），入库退库冲销查询则该字段为入库记录id（H1019返回的入库记录id），移库冲销查询则该字段为移出库房记录id（H1035服务返回的移出记录id） |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| category |  | int | **√** | |  | 类别：0-非中草药;1-中草药 (根据部门性质来判断是否是中草药和非中草药,有中药房中药库性质的部门传入1;反之传入 0:默认为0 |
| show\_unit |  | int | **√** | |  | 显示单位：0-采购单位;1-售价单位默认为1 |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |

| 1、查询药品外购入库编辑。  2、适用于三方系统进行查询外购入库编辑 | | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "id":"",  "org\_id":"",  "category":1,  "show\_unit":"0"  } | | | | | | |

## 3.9H1025药品外购入库退库查询

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **H1025** | | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **H1025药品外购入库退库查询（V1.0）** | | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/drug/Stock/GetDrugStockListOut** | | | | | |
| **功能简述** | **药品外购入库退库查询** | | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | | |
| 1、药品外购入库退库查询。  2、适用于三方系统进行药品外购入库退库查询 | | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "storehouse\_id": "string",  "org\_id": "string",  "keyword": "string",  "business\_unit": 0,  "product\_id": "string",  "is\_drug": 0,  "is\_mc": 0,  "is\_in\_stock": 0,  "is\_share": 0,  "supplier\_id": "string",  "is\_lot": 0  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| storehouse\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 库房id |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| keyword |  | string | **√** | |  | 输入药品参数(简码,名称检索) |
| business\_unit |  | string | **√** | |  | 药品单位，1：售价单位，0：药库单位 |
| product\_id |  | string |  | |  | 产品id |
| is\_drug |  | int | **√** | |  | 录入药品，传1 |
| is\_mc |  | int | **√** | |  | 录入卫材，传1 |
| is\_in\_stock |  | int | **√** | |  | 仅查看有库存的药品，1：查询有库存，0：所有 |
| is\_share |  | int | **√** | |  | 是否仅显示共用 默认0-代表显示所有;1代表仅显示共用 |
| supplier\_id |  | string |  | |  | 供应商id（入库退库必传，移库可不用传） |
| is\_lot |  | int |  | |  | 用于退库时查询供应商为空和不分批的数据，传1会查询供应商为空和不分批数据，0是只根据供应商查询，默认0 |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "code": 200,  "msg": "",  "data": [  {  "storehouse": "西药房",  "storehouse\_id": "500543d0dc6cc788",  "lot\_no": "0056",  "lot": "20220523144921002",  "production\_date": null,  "sourceland": "",  "supplier\_id": "",  "supplier": "",  "expiry\_date": "2022-06-05 00:00:00",  "variety\_id": "5ec9645ec5f1dc60",  "source": "",  "essential\_drugs\_code": "",  "purchase\_unit": "",  "purchase\_unit\_coefficient": 1,  "max\_expiry": 24,  "is\_pharmacy\_batch": 1,  "is\_storehouse\_batch": 1,  "is\_change": 1,  "approval\_no": "",  "price\_level": "",  "brief\_code": "999GMLKL",  "category": "5",  "category\_name": "",  "drug\_id": "85f9c6c077702b6a",  "code": "052601",  "country\_code": "",  "country\_norm\_name": "",  "platform\_code": "",  "platform\_name": "",  "name": "999感冒灵颗粒",  "brand\_name": "",  "strength": "粒",  "manufacturer": "",  "supplier\_name": "东拉西扯",  "unit": "粒",  "cost\_price": 3,  "price": 3,  "usable\_qty": 5,  "actual\_qty": 5,  "actual\_charge": 15,  "actual\_cost": 15,  "actual\_spread": 0  }  ],  "timestamp": 1695277069,  "innermsg": ""  } | | | | | | |

# 药品移库数据接口详情示例

## 4.1H1028药品移库单新增提交

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **H1028** | | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **H1028药品移库单新增提交（V1.0）** | | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/drug/DrugShift/AddDrugShift** | | | | | |
| **功能简述** | **药品移库单新增提交** | | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | | |
| 1、药品移库单新增提交。  2、适用于三方系统进行药品移库单新增提交 | | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "org\_id": "string",  "no": "string",  "other\_org\_id": "string",  "other\_org\_name": "string",  "storehouse\_id": "string",  "storehouse": "string",  "other\_dept\_id": "string",  "bill\_type": 201,  "other\_dept": "string",  "creator": "string",  "apply\_id": 0,  "show\_unit": 0,  "category": 0,  "description": "string",  "list\_detail": [  {  "sno": 0,  "drug\_id": "string",  "lot\_no": "string",  "lot": "string",  "approval\_no": "string",  "manufacturer": "string",  "supplier\_id": "string",  "production\_date": "2023-09-21T08:27:13.948Z",  "expiry\_date": "2023-09-21T08:27:13.948Z",  "qty": 0,  "actual\_qty": 0,  "unit": "string",  "business\_unit": "string",  "cost\_price": 0,  "cost": 0,  "price": 0,  "price\_charge": 0,  "spread": 0,  "business\_qty": 0,  "business\_cost\_price": 0,  "business\_price": 0,  "apply\_detail\_id": 0  }  ]  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| no |  | string |  | |  | 单据号,新增不填，传空，修改时必传（H1033服务返回的单据号no） |
| other\_org\_id |  | string |  | |  | 调入机构id 调拨时必填,移库时为空 |
| other\_org\_name |  | string |  | |  | 调入机构名称 外部调拨时必填,其他可选填 |
| storehouse\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 移出库房ID |
| storehouse |  | string | **√** | |  | 移出库房名称 |
| other\_dept\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 移入库房ID |
| other\_dept |  | string | **√** | |  | 移入库房名称 |
| bill\_type |  | string | **√** | |  | 单据类型：传304 |
| creator |  | string | **√** | |  | 填制人名称 |
| apply\_id |  | string |  | |  | 申领id(申领单转调拨单据时不允许为空,直接新增调拨单据时为空) |
| show\_unit |  | int | **√** | |  | 显示单位，1：售价单位，0：药库单位默认1 |
| category |  | int | **√** | |  | 类别：0-非中草药;1-中草药 (根据部门性质来判断是否是中草药和非中草药,有中药房中药库性质的部门传入1;反之传入 0:默认为0 |
| description |  | string |  | |  | 摘要 |
| list\_detail |  | string |  | |  | 单据明细 |
| sno | list\_detail | int | **√** | |  | 序号 |
| drug\_id | list\_detail | string | **√** | |  | 药品id |
| lot\_no | list\_detail | string | **√** | |  | 批号 |
| lot | list\_detail | string | **√** | |  | 批次 |
| approval\_no | list\_detail | string |  | |  | 批准文号 |

## 4.6H1033药品移库移出记录

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **H1033** | | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **H1033药品移库移出记录（V1.0）** | | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/drug/DrugShift/GetDrugShiftOut** | | | | | |

| 1、药品移库移出记录。  2、适用于三方系统进行查询药品移库移出记录 | | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "org\_id": "string",  "storehouse\_id": "string",  "no": "string",  "not\_audit": 0,  "s\_create\_time": "2023-09-22T01:12:47.802Z",  "e\_create\_time": "2023-09-22T01:12:47.802Z",  "is\_audit": 0,  "s\_audit\_time": "2023-09-22T01:12:47.802Z",  "e\_audit\_time": "2023-09-22T01:12:47.802Z",  "writeoff": 0,  "creator": "string",  "auditor": "string",  "drug\_id": "string",  "supplier\_id": "string",  "page\_num": 0,  "page\_size": 0,  "product\_id": "string"  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| storehouse\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 库房id（移出库房id） |
| no |  | string |  | |  | 单据号 |
| not\_audit |  | int |  | |  | 未审核，配合填制时间使用，若输入了填制开始结束时间，该参数传1，否则传0 |
| s\_create\_time |  | string |  | |  | 填制开始日期 |
| e\_create\_time |  | string |  | |  | 填制结束日期 |
| is\_audit |  | int |  | |  | 已审核，配合审核时间使用，若输入了审核开始结束时间，该参数传1，否则传0 |
| s\_audit\_time |  | string |  | |  | 审核开始日期 |
| e\_audit\_time |  | string |  | |  | 审核结束日期 |
| writeoff |  | int |  | |  | 是否冲销，1：选择后查询冲销负记录，0：不显示冲销负记录 |
| creator |  | string |  | |  | 填制人名称 |
| auditor |  | string |  | |  | 审核人名称 |
| drug\_id |  | string |  | |  | 药品id |
| supplier\_id |  | string |  | |  | 供应商id |
| page\_num |  | int | **√** | |  | 当前第几页 |
| page\_size |  | int | **√** | |  | 一页多少条数据 |
| product\_id |  | string |  | |  | 产品id |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "code": 200,  "msg": "",  "data": {  "sum": {  "cost\_gap": 0,  "price\_charge": 22,  "cost": 22,  "spread": 0  },  "Total": 2,  "PageList": [  {  "id": "5561016985007139990",  "no": "2309000004",  "shift\_storehouse": "西药库",  "cost": 2,  "price\_charge": 2,  "spread": 0,  "creator": "管理员",  "create\_time": "2023-09-22 09:08:41",  "receiver": "管理员",  "receive\_time": "2023-09-22 09:09:32",  "drug\_preparer": "",  "send\_time": null,  "rec\_status": 0,  "description": "",  "audit\_suggestion": "",  "shift\_storehouse\_id": "474a4fca4643f3b4",  "bill\_sign": 0,  "apply\_id": "0",  "reversal\_mark": "",  "bill\_type": "",  "status": 1  }  ]  },  "timestamp": 1695346161,  "innermsg": ""  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **数组** | **说明** | | |
| code |  | int |  | 返回结果: 200-成功; 500-失败 | | |
| msg |  | string |  | 返回信息 | | |
| data |  |  |  | 执行结果 | | |

# 物资供应商数据接口详情示例

## W1001A查询物资供应商信息

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **W1001A** | | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **W1001A查询物资供应商（V1.0）** | | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/GetMatlSupperList** | | | | | |
| **功能简述** | **查询物资供应商** | | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | | |
| 1、查询物资供应商 | | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {     **"org\_id"**: **""**,     **"keyword"**: **""** } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| keyword |  | String |  | |  | 关键字（编码/名称/简码） |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |

| creator | matl\_info | string |  | |  | 创建人 |
| status | matl\_info | string |  | |  | 状态，1-审核；0-未审核 |

| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **数组** | **说明** | | |
| code |  | int |  | 返回结果: 200-成功; 500-失败 | | |
| msg |  | string |  | 返回信息 | | |

## **11.1H1040处方发药未发放查询**

| is\_uncharged\_drug\_send | list\_data | int | **√** |  | 允许未收费的门诊划价处方发药 :0-不允许;1-允许 |
| show\_unit | list\_data | int | **√** |  | 药品单位，1：售价单位，0：业务单位，默认1 |

| drug\_id | drug\_details | string | **√** |  | 药品id |

| single | drug\_details | number |  |  | 单量 |

| freq | drug\_details | string |  |  | 频次 |
| tcm\_decoct | drug\_details | string |  |  | 中药煎法 |

| sub\_sno | drug\_details | int |  |  | 子序号 |
| entrust | drug\_details | string |  |  | 嘱托 |
| footnote | drug\_details | string |  |  | 脚注 |
| category | drug\_details | int |  |  | 药品类别 4-卫材;5-西药;6-中成药;7-中草药 |
| is\_trace | drug\_details | int |  |  | 跟踪在用 卫材传入是否跟踪再用属性,药品类的默认传入1 |
| exec\_class | drug\_details | int |  |  | 给药途径分类：0-未明确,1-输液类,2-注射类;3-口服类，仅给药途径使用 |
| prop | drug\_details | int |  |  | 医嘱效期：0-临嘱；1-长嘱 |
| give\_mode | drug\_details | int |  |  | 发药方式：4-正常 5-外购药 6-自备药(外) 7-离院带药 8-自取药 9-自备药（内） 10-不计费 11-分组药 |
| bar\_code | drug\_details | string |  |  | 追溯条码:主要用于记录高值耗材追溯条码 |
| give\_source\_code | drug\_details | int |  |  | 1：门诊，2：住院 |
| **出参示例** | | | | | |

| create\_org\_id | drug\_info | string |  |  | 创建机构id |
| price | drug\_info | number | **√** |  | 售价 |
| is\_share | drug\_info | int | **√** |  | 是否共用 1-是;0-否 |
| income\_item\_id | drug\_info | string | **√** |  | 收入科目（H1048获取的收入科目id） |

| is\_hvc | drug\_info | int |  |  | 是否高值耗材 |

| name | variety\_info | string | **√** |  | 通用名（同drug\_info中的name一致） |
| py\_code | variety\_info | string | **√** |  | 拼音码 |
| wb\_code | variety\_info | string |  |  | 五笔码 |
| dosage\_unit | variety\_info | string | **√** |  | 剂量单位 |
| form | variety\_info | string | **√** |  | 剂型，没得默认传19 |
| toxicology\_class | variety\_info | string |  |  | 毒理分类：1-麻醉药;2-毒性药;3-精神I类;4-精神II类;5-普通药（没得默认传5） |
| value\_class | variety\_info | string |  |  | 价值分类：1-普价;2-贵重;3-昂贵 |
| recipe\_limit | variety\_info | number |  |  | 处方限量 |
| recipe\_grade | variety\_info | string |  |  | 处方职级 |
| insurance\_grade | variety\_info | string |  |  | 医保职级 |

| is\_generics | variety\_info | int |  |  | 是否通过评价的仿制药 |
| is\_import\_original | variety\_info | int |  |  | 是否是进口原研药 |
| anti\_type | variety\_info | int |  |  | 抗菌药物：1-非限制使用；2-限制使用；3-特殊使用 |
| is\_hormone | variety\_info | int |  |  | 激素类药 |
| is\_no\_bulk | variety\_info | int | **√** |  | 无散药，是否不存在散装饮片,传1，默认不添加散药，添加的话直接在drug\_info中传入 |
| is\_package | variety\_info | int |  |  | 是否包装饮片 |
| is\_avoid\_decoct | variety\_info | int |  |  | 是否免煎饮片 |
| service\_object | variety\_info | string | **√** |  | 服务对象：1-门诊；2-住院；3-体检； 存储集合，多个用逗号隔开 |
| creator | variety\_info | string |  |  | 建档人 |
| org\_id | variety\_info | string |  |  | 私有才传入机构id |
| use\_limit | variety\_info | number |  |  | 使用限量 |
| limit\_cycle | variety\_info | int |  |  | 限量周期 |
| apply\_range | variety\_info | int | **√** |  | 适用范围,用于社区中心和村医是否共用项目;0-中心和村医共用;1-不适用于村医; |
| status | variety\_info | int |  |  | 0-未审核;1正常;-1停用（传1） |
| create\_org\_id | variety\_info | string | **√** |  | 创建机构id |
| is\_prescription | variety\_info | int |  |  | 是否处方用药:0-非处方用药,1-处方用药 |
| is\_share | variety\_info | int | **√** |  | is\_share:是否共用 1-是;0-否 |
| is\_all\_org | variety\_info | int | **√** |  | 是否适用于所有机构 1-是;0-否 |
| tcm\_type | variety\_info | int |  |  | 型态标识：0-普通;1-制剂;2-协定药;3-免煎饮片;4-包装饮片 |
| purchase\_unit | variety\_info | string | **√** |  | 采购单位（同drug\_info中的purchase\_unit一致） |
| unit | variety\_info | string | **√** |  | 售价单位（同drug\_info中的purchase\_unit一致） |
| dosage\_coefficient | variety\_info | number | **√** |  | 剂量系数（用于规格售价单位显示） |
| purchase\_unit\_base | variety\_info | int | **√** |  | 采购包装基数（同drug\_info中的purchase\_unit\_base一致） |
| purchase\_unit\_coefficient | variety\_info | int | **√** |  | 采购单位系数（同drug\_info中的purchase\_unit\_coefficient一致） |
| is\_change | variety\_info | int | **√** |  | 是否变价 1-是（时价）;0-否（定价） |
| limit\_price | variety\_info | number |  |  | 采购限价 |
| cost\_price | variety\_info | number | **√** |  | 成本价（同drug\_info中的cost\_price一致） |
| price | variety\_info | number | **√** |  | 售价（同drug\_info中的price一致） |

|  | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | |
| {     **"id"**: **""**,     **"parent\_id"**: **"string"**,     **"code"**: **"string"**,     **"name"**: **"string"**,     **"py\_code"**: **"string"**,     **"category"**: **0**,     **"prop"**: **0** } | | | | | |

| prop |  | int | **√** |  | category=4-卫材时:1-低值耗材分类;2-高值耗材分类,其余传0 |
| **出参示例** | | | | | |
| {  "code": 200,  "msg": "查询成功",  "data": null,  "timestamp": 1701691489,  "innermsg": ""  } | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **数组** | **说明** | |
| code |  | int |  | 返回结果: 200-成功; 500-失败 | |
| msg |  | string |  | 返回信息 | |
| data |  |  |  | 返回数据 | |

# 药品进销存数据接口详情示例

## A4001商品盘存上传

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **A4001** | | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **A4001商品盘存上传（V1.0）** | | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/drug/GetInventoryInfo** | | | | | |
| **功能简述** | **根据开始、结束时间及机构查询所有药品盘点数据信息** | | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | | |
| 1. 查询药品盘点信息。 2. 适用于三方系统进行新增盘点数据 | | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "org\_id": "",  "start\_time": "",  "end\_time": ""  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| start\_time |  | string | **√** | |  | 开始时间 |
| end\_time |  | string | **√** | |  | 结束时间 |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "code": "200",  "msg": "查询商品盘存上传信息成功！",  "data": [  {  "prod\_stoin\_id": "5013090517888055513",  "prod\_type": 1,  "med\_list\_codg": "280103",  "fixmedins\_hilist\_id": "zlsoft",  "fixmedins\_hilist\_name": "中联区卫",  "rx\_flag": "",  "invdate": "2023-08-21 11:28:11",  "ord\_no": "2308000002",  "inv\_cnt": 1,  "pric": 19,  "spler\_code": null,  "spler\_name": null,  "manu\_lotnum": "",  "batch\_number": "0",  "fixmedins\_bchno": "0(307-2308000002)",  "manu\_date": null,  "expy\_end": null,  "storageroomname": "测试药房",  "stockstatus": 1,  "memo": ""  }  ]  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **数组** | **说明** | | |
| code |  | int |  | 返回结果: 200-成功; 500-失败 | | |
| msg |  | string |  | 返回信息 | | |
| data |  |  |  | 执行结果: 返回查询的盘点信息数据 | | |
| prod\_stoin\_id | data | string |  | 商品入库记录主键, 院内惟一 | | |
| prod\_type | data | int |  | 商品类型1、药品2、耗材、3、器械 | | |
| med\_list\_codg | data | string |  | 医疗目录编码 | | |
| fixmedins\_hilist\_id | data | string |  | 定点医药机构目录编号 | | |
| fixmedins\_hilist\_name | data | string |  | 定点医药机构目录名称 | | |
| rx\_flag | data | string |  | 处方药标志 | | |
| invdate | data | string |  | 盘存日期 | | |
| ord\_no | data | string |  | 订单号,如在省公共资源交易中心采购-订单号，否则不用 | | |
| inv\_cnt | data | number |  | 库存数量,按最小计价包装单位统计 | | |
| pric | data | number |  | 单价 | | |
| spler\_code | data | string |  | 供应商编码,指配送企业编码 | | |
| spler\_name | data | string |  | 供应商名称,指配送企业名称 | | |
| manu\_lotnum | data | string |  | 生产批号 | | |
| batch\_number | data | string |  | 批次号,同品、同批用作销售的 | | |
| fixmedins\_bchno | data | string |  | 定点医药机构批次流水号,医药机构自定义批次号 | | |
| manu\_date | data | string |  | 生产日期 | | |
| expy\_end | data | string |  | 有效期止 | | |
| storageroomname | data | string |  | 库房名称 | | |
| stockstatus | data | int |  | 库存状态,库存状态，1 正常、2 缺货、3 停止挂网 | | |
| memo | data | string |  | 备注 | | |

| end\_time |  | string | **√** |  | 结束时间 |

| fixmedins\_hilist\_id | data | string |  | 定点医药机构目录编号 | | |
| fixmedins\_hilist\_name | data | string |  | 定点医药机构目录名称 | | |
| receivedeptcode | data | string |  | 领用科室编码 | | |
| receivedeptname | data | string |  | 领用科室 | | |
| receiveusername | data | string |  | 领用人 | | |
| receivetime | data | string |  | 领用时间 | | |
| receiveno | data | number |  | 领用数量 | | |
| med\_list\_codg | data | string |  | 医疗目录编码 | | |

# 药品申领数据接口详情示例

## 2.2H1001获取药品库存信息

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **H1001** | | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **H1001获取药品库存信息 （V1.0）** | | | | | |

| **功能简述** | **查询药品库存信息** | | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | | |

## 2.4H1003药品申领单新增提交

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **H1003** | | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **H1003药品申领单新增提交（V1.0）** | | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/drug/DrugApply/AddDrugApply** | | | | | |
| **功能简述** | **药品申领单新增** | | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | | |
| 1、药品申领单新增。  2、适用于三方系统进行药品申领单新增 | | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "id": 0,  "no": "string",  "org\_id": "string",  "other\_org\_id": "string",  "apply\_dept\_id": "string",  "apply\_dept": "string",  "storehouse\_id": "string",  "storehouse": "string",  "description": "string",  "creator": "string",  "is\_employ": 0,  "is\_external": 0,  "is\_show\_unit": 0,  "list\_apply\_detail": [  {  "drug\_id": "string",  "app\_qty": 0,  "lot\_no": "string",  "lot": "string"  }  ]  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| id |  | string |  | |  | 申领记录id,新增不填，传空，修改时必传 |
| no |  | string | **√** | |  | 单据号,新增不填，传空，修改时必传 |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| other\_org\_id |  | string |  | |  | 对方机构id，在向上级机构领用时需要 |
| apply\_dept\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 申领部门ID |

| is\_external |  | int |  | |  | 是否向外部申领:0-否;1-是，传0 |
| is\_show\_unit |  | int | **√** | |  | 显示单位，1：售价单位，0：药库单位 |
| list\_apply\_detail |  |  |  | |  | 单据明细 |

| **出参示例** | | | | | | |

| page\_size |  | int | **√** | |  | 一页多少条数据 |

| {  "code": 200,  "msg": "",  "data": "2309000002",  "timestamp": 1695112218,  "innermsg": ""  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **数组** | **说明** | | |
| code |  | int |  | 返回结果: 200-成功; 500-失败 | | |
| msg |  | string |  | 返回信息 | | |
| data |  |  |  | 执行结果，返回单据号 | | |

## 2.13H1012药品领用单冲销单据查询

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |

| **服务名称** | **H1012药品领用单冲销单据查询（V1.0）** | | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/drug/DrugBillStrikes/GetDrugStrikes** | | | | | |
| **功能简述** | **药品领用单冲销单据查询** | | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | | |
| 1、药品领用单冲销单据查询。  2、适用于三方系统进行药品领用单冲销单据查询 | | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "id":"",  "org\_id":"",  "category":0,  "show\_unit":"1"  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| id |  | string | **√** | |  | 领用记录id（H1009返回的领用记录id），入库退库冲销查询则该字段为入库记录id（H1019返回的入库记录id），移库冲销查询则该字段为移出库房记录id（H1035服务返回的移出记录id） |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| category |  | int | **√** | |  | 类别：0-非中草药;1-中草药 (根据部门性质来判断是否是中草药和非中草药,有中药房中药库性质的部门传入1;反之传入 0:默认为0 |
| show\_unit |  | int | **√** | |  | 显示单位：0-采购单位;1-售价单位默认为1 |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "code": 200,  "msg": "",  "data": [  {  "name": "0419同步感冒药",  "strength": "10\*1",  "source": "",  "unit": "盒",  "purchase\_unit": "",  "sno": 1,  "drug\_id": "32ddca3374e29470",  "lot": "20220810150109001",  "lot\_no": "12132432",  "manufacturer": "上海科邦医用乳胶器材有限公司",  "expiry\_date": "2024-08-10 00:00:00",  "rec\_status": 0,  "sourceland": "",  "approval\_no": "",  "residue\_qty": 5,  "qty": 0,  "purchase\_limit\_price": 0,  "cost\_price": 2,  "cost": 10,  "price": 2,  "price\_charge": 10,  "spread": 0,  "distribute\_no": "",  "invoice\_no": "",  "production\_date": "2022-08-10 00:00:00"  }  ],  "timestamp": 1695175964,  "innermsg": ""  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **数组** | **说明** | | |
| code |  | int |  | 返回结果: 200-成功; 500-失败 | | |
| msg |  | string |  | 返回信息 | | |
| data |  |  |  | 执行结果 | | |

## 2.15H1014药品申领单修改提交

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **服务编码** | **H1014** | | | | | |
| **服务名称** | **H1014药品申领单修改提交（V1.0）** | | | | | |
| **服务地址** | **instance/publish/yhis/V1/drug/DrugApply/UpdateDrugApply** | | | | | |
| **功能简述** | **药品申领单修改** | | | | | |
| **详细描述（应用场景、数据处理逻辑描述）** | | | | | | |
| 1、药品申领单修改。  2、适用于三方系统进行药品申领单修改 | | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "id": 0,  "no": "string",  "org\_id": "string",  "other\_org\_id": "string",  "apply\_dept\_id": "string",  "apply\_dept": "string",  "storehouse\_id": "string",  "storehouse": "string",  "description": "string",  "creator": "string",  "is\_employ": 0,  "is\_external": 0,  "is\_show\_unit": 0,  "list\_apply\_detail": [  {  "drug\_id": "string",  "app\_qty": 0,  "lot\_no": "string",  "lot": "string"  }  ]  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| id |  | string | **√** | |  | 申领记录id,新增不填，传空，修改时必传(H1002服务返回的id) |
| no |  | string | **√** | |  | 单据号,新增不填，传空，修改时必传 |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| other\_org\_id |  | string |  | |  | 对方机构id，在向上级机构领用时需要 |
| apply\_dept\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 申领部门ID |
| apply\_dept |  | string | **√** | |  | 申领部门 |
| storehouse\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 发药库房ID |
| storehouse |  | string | **√** | |  | 发药库房名称 |
| description |  | string |  | |  | 摘要 |
| creator |  | string | **√** | |  | 填制人名称 |
| is\_employ |  | int | **√** | |  | 是否领用:0-移库;1-领用 |
| is\_external |  | int |  | |  | 是否向外部申领:0-否;1-是 |
| is\_show\_unit |  | int | **√** | |  | 显示单位，1：售价单位，0：药库单位 |
| list\_apply\_detail |  |  |  | |  | 单据明细 |
| drug\_id | list\_apply\_detail | string | **√** | |  | 药品ID |
| app\_qty | list\_apply\_detail | number | **√** | |  | 填写数量 |
| lot\_no | list\_apply\_detail | string |  | |  | 批号 |
| lot | list\_apply\_detail | string |  | |  | 批次 |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |

| msg |  | string |  | 返回信息 | | |
| data |  |  |  | 执行结果 | | |

| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| id |  | string | **√** | |  | 入库记录id,新增不填，传空，修改时必传（H1017返回的入库记录id字段） |

| storehouse\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 发药库房ID |
| storehouse |  | string | **√** | |  | 发药库房名称 |

| category |  | int |  | |  | 类别：0-非中草药;1-中草药 (根据部门性质来判断是否是中草药和非中草药,有中药房中药库性质的部门传入1;反之传入 0:默认为0 |

## 3.5H1019药品外购入库记录

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |

| 1、药品外购入库记录。  2、适用于三方系统进行查询药品外购入库记录 | | | | | | |
| **入参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "org\_id": "string",  "storehouse\_id": "string",  "s\_create\_time": "",  "e\_create\_time": "",  "s\_audit\_time": "",  "e\_audit\_time": "",  "creator": "",  "auditor": "",  "no\_sign": 0,  "no": "",  "drug\_id": "",  "is\_audit": 0,  "not\_audit": 0,  "page\_num": 0,  "page\_size": 0,  "is\_strike": 0,  "product\_id": ""  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **必填** | | **数组** | **说明** |
| org\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 机构id |
| storehouse\_id |  | string | **√** | |  | 库房id |

| e\_create\_time |  | string |  | |  | 填制结束日期 |

| e\_audit\_time |  | string |  | |  | 审核结束日期 |

| auditor |  | string |  | |  | 审核人名称 |

| no |  | string |  | |  | 单据号，no\_sign=1该条件生效 |
| drug\_id |  | string |  | |  | 药品id |
| is\_audit |  | int |  | |  | 已审核，配合审核时间使用，若输入了审核开始结束时间，该参数传1，否则传0 |
| not\_audit |  | int |  | |  | 未审核，配合填制时间使用，若输入了填制开始结束时间，该参数传1，否则传0 |
| page\_num |  | int | **√** | |  | 当前第几页 |
| page\_size |  | int | **√** | |  | 一页多少条数据 |
| is\_strike |  | int |  | |  | 是否冲销，1：选择后查询冲销负记录，0：不显示冲销负记录 |
| product\_id |  | string |  | |  | 产品id |
| supplier\_id |  | string |  | |  | 供应商id |
| category |  | int | **√** | |  | 类别：0-非中草药;1-中草药 (根据部门性质来判断是否是中草药和非中草药,有中药房中药库性质的部门传入1;反之传入 0:默认为0 |
| **出参示例** | | | | | | |
| {  "code": 200,  "msg": "查询成功!",  "data": {  "sum": {  "cost\_gap": 0,  "price\_charge": 2,  "cost": 2,  "spread": 0  },  "Total": 1,  "PageList": [  {  "id": "4922667338506204270",  "no": "2309000001",  "other\_dept": "住院内科",  "cost": 2,  "price\_charge": 2,  "spread": 0,  "creator": "管理员",  "create\_time": "2023-09-19 16:15:32",  "auditor": "",  "audit\_time": null,  "rec\_status": 0,  "description": "【原申领单号：2309000003】",  "audit\_suggestion": "",  "other\_dept\_id": "ddaee6a44fd6e5fc",  "bill\_sign": 0,  "apply\_id": "5233451538145882856",  "charge\_against": "",  "recipient": "七七1",  "status": 0  }  ]  },  "timestamp": 1695263158,  "innermsg": ""  } | | | | | | |
| **节点** | **父节点** | **类型** | **数组** | **说明** | | |
| code |  | int |  | 返回结果: 200-成功; 500-失败 | | |
| msg |  | string |  | 返回信息 | | |
| data |  |  |  | 执行结果 | | |
